 5136   
 5137   void minimizeTV2(const emlrtStack *sp, emxArray_real32_T *f, real_T tvConstant,
 5138                    real_T nIterTV)
 5139   {
 5140     int32_T i;
 5141     emxArray_real_T *f_grad;
 5142     emxArray_real_T *x;
 5143     emxArray_real_T *b_x;
 5144     emxArray_real_T *c_x;
 5145     boolean_T overflow;
 5146     boolean_T p;
 5147     int32_T k;
 5148     uint32_T sz[3];
 5149     int32_T vlen;
 5150     int32_T npages;
 5151     int32_T b_k;
 5152     int32_T b_i;
 5153     int32_T xoffset;
 5154     real_T s;
 5155     int32_T b_f[3];
 5156     int32_T b_f_grad[3];
 5157     emlrtStack st;
 5158     emlrtStack b_st;
 5159     emlrtStack c_st;
 5160     emlrtStack d_st;
 5161     emlrtStack e_st;
 5162     st.prev = sp;
 5163     st.tls = sp->tls;
 5164     b_st.prev = &st;
 5165     b_st.tls = st.tls;
 5166     c_st.prev = &b_st;
 5167     c_st.tls = b_st.tls;
 5168     d_st.prev = &c_st;
 5169     d_st.tls = c_st.tls;
 5170     e_st.prev = &d_st;
 5171     e_st.tls = d_st.tls;
 5172     emlrtHeapReferenceStackEnterFcnR2012b(sp);
 5173     emlrtForLoopVectorCheckR2012b(1.0, 1.0, nIterTV, mxDOUBLE_CLASS, (int32_T)
 5174       nIterTV, (emlrtRTEInfo *)&p_emlrtRTEI, sp);
 5175     i = 0;
 5176     emxInit_real_T(sp, &f_grad, 3, &i_emlrtRTEI, true);
 5177     emxInit_real_T(sp, &x, 3, &emlrtRTEI, true);
 5178     emxInit_real_T(sp, &b_x, 3, &emlrtRTEI, true);
 5179     emxInit_real_T(sp, &c_x, 3, &emlrtRTEI, true);
 5180     while (i <= (int32_T)nIterTV - 1) {
 5181       st.site = &emlrtRSI;
 5182       tvGradient(&st, f, f_grad);
 5183       st.site = &b_emlrtRSI;
 5184       b_power(&st, f_grad, x);
 5185       st.site = &b_emlrtRSI;
 5186       b_st.site = &p_emlrtRSI;
 5187       if (((x->size[0] == 1) && (x->size[1] == 1) && (x->size[2] == 1)) ||
 5188           (x->size[0] != 1)) {
 5189         overflow = true;
 5190       } else {
 5191         overflow = false;
 5192       }
 5193   
 5194       if (!overflow) {
 5195         emlrtErrorWithMessageIdR2012b(&b_st, &n_emlrtRTEI,
 5196           "Coder:toolbox:autoDimIncompatibility", 0);
 5197       }
 5198   
 5199       overflow = false;
 5200       p = false;
 5201       if ((x->size[0] != 0) || (x->size[1] != 0) || (x->size[2] != 1)) {
 5202       } else {
 5203         p = true;
 5204       }
 5205   
 5206       if (p) {
 5207         overflow = true;
 5208       }
 5209   
 5210       if (overflow) {
 5211         emlrtErrorWithMessageIdR2012b(&b_st, &o_emlrtRTEI,
 5212           "Coder:toolbox:UnsupportedSpecialEmpty", 0);
 5213       }
 5214   
 5215       c_st.site = &q_emlrtRSI;
 5216       for (k = 0; k < 3; k++) {
 5217         sz[k] = (uint32_T)x->size[k];
 5218       }
 5219   
 5220       k = b_x->size[0] * b_x->size[1] * b_x->size[2];
 5221       b_x->size[0] = 1;
 5222       b_x->size[1] = (int32_T)sz[1];
 5223       b_x->size[2] = (int32_T)sz[2];
 5224       emxEnsureCapacity(&c_st, (emxArray__common *)b_x, k, sizeof(real_T),
 5225                         &emlrtRTEI);
 5226       if ((x->size[0] == 0) || (x->size[1] == 0) || (x->size[2] == 0)) {
 5227         k = b_x->size[0] * b_x->size[1] * b_x->size[2];
 5228         b_x->size[0] = 1;
 5229         emxEnsureCapacity(&c_st, (emxArray__common *)b_x, k, sizeof(real_T),
 5230                           &emlrtRTEI);
 5231         b_i = b_x->size[2];
 5232         for (k = 0; k < b_i; k++) {
 5233           xoffset = b_x->size[1];
 5234           for (vlen = 0; vlen < xoffset; vlen++) {
